information</label></div></div><div class="feedback-dialog__choice" data-stats-id="send-helpcenter-feedback-radio"><div class="material-radio"><input class="material-radio__input" id="helpcenter-feedback-radio" name="feedback-choice" value="HELPCENTER" type="radio"><label class="material-radio__label-text" for="helpcenter-feedback-radio" role="presentation"><div class="material-radio__circle" aria-hidden="true"></div><div class="material-radio__fill" aria-hidden="true"></div>General Help Center experience</label></div></div></div><div class="material-dialog__actions"><button class="material2-button" data-material-dialog-action="next">Next</button></div></div><div data-stats-ve="32"><div class="appbar-scroll-box"><div class="appbar-container"><div class="appbar"><div class="appbar-internal"><div><a class="appbar-helpcenter-sections__link appbar-helpcenter-sections--helpcenter appbar-helpcenter-sections--active" aria-label="Help Center" aria-selected="true" href="/chrome/?hl=en">Help Center</a><a class="appbar-helpcenter-sections__link appbar-helpcenter-sections--community" aria-selected="false" href="/chrome/community?hl=en">Community</a></div><div class="appbar-links"><span class="appbar-icon appbar-link-container"><a class="product-icon" data-stats-ve="36" href="//www.google.com/chrome" target="_blank"><span itemprop="title">Google Chrome</span><svg viewbox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M19 19H5V5h7V3H5c-1.11 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.89 2 2 2h14c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2v-7h-2v7zM14 3v2h3.59l-9.83 9.83 1.41 1.41L19 6.41V10h2V3h-7z"></path></svg></a></span>    </div></div></div></div></div></div>   </header> <div class="hcfe-content" role="main">  <section class="primary-container"> <div class="page-width-container">    <div class="main-content">     <article class="article page" sc-render-smart-button="false" itemscope=""> <section class="article-container" data-stats-ve="35"><h1>Start or stop automatically reporting errors &amp; crashes</h1><div class="article-content-container"><div class="cc"><p>Allowing Chrome to send us automatic reports helps us prioritize what to fix and improve in Chrome. These reports can include things like when Chrome crashes, how much memory you’re using, and some personal information.</p>

<p>You can start or stop allowing these reports any time.</p>


<gkms-context-selector id="7182441"></gkms-context-selector><div class="zippy-wrapper">
  <h2 class="zippy">Computer</h2>

  <div>
    <ol>
      <li>On your computer, open Chrome.</li>
      <li>At the top right, click More <img src="//lh3.googleusercontent.com/E2q6Vj9j60Dw0Z6NZFEx5vSB9yoZJp7C8suuvQXVA_2weMCXstGD7JEvNrzX3wuQrPtL=w36-h36" width="18" height="18" alt="More" title="More" data-mime-type="image/png" data-alt-src="//lh3.googleusercontent.com/E2q6Vj9j60Dw0Z6NZFEx5vSB9yoZJp7C8suuvQXVA_2weMCXstGD7JEvNrzX3wuQrPtL">&nbsp;<img src="//lh3.googleusercontent.com/3_l97rr0GvhSP2XV5OoCkV2ZDTIisAOczrSdzNCBxhIKWrjXjHucxNwocghoUa39gw=w36-h36" width="18" height="18" alt="and then" title="and then" data-mime-type="image/png" data-alt-src="//lh3.googleusercontent.com/3_l97rr0GvhSP2XV5OoCkV2ZDTIisAOczrSdzNCBxhIKWrjXjHucxNwocghoUa39gw">&nbsp;<strong>Settings</strong>.</li>
      <li>Under “You and Google,” select&nbsp;<strong>Sync and Google services</strong>.</li>
      <li>Turn on or off <strong>Help improve Chrome's features and performance</strong>.</li>
    </ol>
  </div>
</div>

<div class="zippy-wrapper">
  <h2 class="zippy">Chromebook</h2>

  <div>
    <ol>
      <li>At the bottom right, select the time.</li>
      <li>Select Settings <img src="//storage.googleapis.com/support-kms-prod/EhnJKCYnCpUVMQvn9LxVpGRY4fJAjUYOfZGt" width="18" height="18" alt="" data-mime-type="image/png">.</li>
      <li>At the bottom, click <strong>Advanced</strong>.</li>
      <li>Under "Privacy and security," turn <strong>Automatically send diagnostic and usage data to Google</strong> on or off.</li>
    </ol>

    <p><strong>Note:</strong> If you’re using your Chromebook at work or school, you might not be able to change this setting. For more help, <a href="https://support.google.com/accounts/answer/6208960" rel="noopener">contact your administrator</a>.</p>
  </div>
</div>



<div></div>

<h2>What these reports include&nbsp;</h2>

<p>If Chrome crashes, some personal information might be included in the report. These reports have:</p>

<ul>
  <li>Memory related to the crash, which may include page contents, payment information, and passwords</li>
  <li>Your Chrome settings</li>
  <li>Extensions you have installed</li>
  <li>The web page you were visiting at the time of the crash</li>
  <li>Your device's operating system, manufacturer, and model</li>
  <li>The country where you’re using Chrome</li>
</ul>

<div></div>

<p>To learn more about what we do with the info from these reports, <a href="https://www.google.com/intl/en/chrome/browser/privacy/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">read Chrome's privacy policy</a>.</p>
